<Date>1571524185645</Date><rate>5<//rate><user_id>106853470786272445883<//user_id>< Text>
Jono's is the place for delicious, fresh sushi in the Corona/Norco. The restaurant is small, cozy, and relaxed with some of the friendliest staff you'll find anywhere. The spicy edamame is a garlicky delight and the Hidden Valley, Johnny Lucas and Lemon rolls were outstanding.

This is not an all-you-can-eat sushi restaurant, which makes me happy, but it is reasonably priced for the quality. If you are looking for smaller bites at a discount they do have happy hours at various times of day.

Jono's is a true find and we're lucky to have them in the area!<//Text>

Most of the staff is not knowledgeable of the products they are selling or offering. The line at the parts counter and register are always backed up with angry costumers having to wait so long! Not professional at all overall. Its sad because Autozone has great parts, prices, and have a highly advanced parts search engine compared to other parts stores.
